    SELECT DISTINCT [a].[IPN_Id], [a].[IPN_No], [a].[IPN_Date], [a].[IPN_StuStaffFlg], [a].[IPN_PushNotification], [c].[AMST_Id], (((CASE
        WHEN [d].[AMST_FirstName] IS NULL
        THEN N' ' ELSE [d].[AMST_FirstName]
    END + N' ') + CASE
        WHEN [d].[AMST_MiddleName] IS NULL
        THEN N' ' ELSE [d].[AMST_MiddleName]
    END) + N' ') + CASE
        WHEN [d].[AMST_LastName] IS NULL
        THEN N' ' ELSE [d].[AMST_LastName]
    END AS [AMST_FirstName], [c].[IPNS_Id], [c].[IPNS_ActiveFlag]
    FROM [IVRM_PushNotification] AS [a]
    CROSS JOIN [IVRM_PushNotification_Student] AS [c]
    CROSS JOIN [Adm_M_Student] AS [d]
    WHERE (((([a].[IPN_Id] = [c].[IPN_Id]) AND ([c].[AMST_Id] = [d].[AMST_Id])) AND ([a].[MI_Id] = @__data_MI_Id_0)) AND ([a].[ASMAY_Id] = @__data_ASMAY_Id_1)) AND ([a].[IPN_Id] = @__data_IPN_Id_2)
) AS [t]
ORDER BY [t].[IPN_Id]" (0723d8ff)
